\doxysubsection*{picomatch}
\label{_amgrpb50aab0af6d7de3ec6663748f3aec961}%
Creates a matcher function from one or more glob patterns.

The returned function takes a string to match as its first argument, and returns true if the string is a match. The returned matcher function also takes a boolean as the second argument that, when true, returns an object with additional information.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{_0drollup_2pluginutils_2dist_2es_2index_8js_a320c9c394b662237be25653cf0ecf4f4}{picomatch}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a4b4eb847520ff4e45de16db801e26133}{require}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'picomatch'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{// picomatch(glob[, options]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{picomatch_8js_aeb1e16ab84300f77d76bd3841ce712f6}{isMatch}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{_0drollup_2pluginutils_2dist_2es_2index_8js_a320c9c394b662237be25653cf0ecf4f4}{picomatch}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'*.!(*a)'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{console.log(\mbox{\hyperlink{picomatch_8js_aeb1e16ab84300f77d76bd3841ce712f6}{isMatch}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'a.a'})); \textcolor{comment}{//=> false}}
\DoxyCodeLine{console.log(\mbox{\hyperlink{picomatch_8js_aeb1e16ab84300f77d76bd3841ce712f6}{isMatch}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'a.b'})); \textcolor{comment}{//=> true}}
\end{DoxyCode}

\hline

\index{rollup.js@{rollup.js}!scan@{scan}}
\index{scan@{scan}!rollup.js@{rollup.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{scan}{scan}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{shared_2rollup_8js_ab94e0a6507d6af3464617b932a6a041a}{picomatch}} scan}



Quickly scans a glob pattern and returns an object with a handful of useful properties, like {\ttfamily is\+Glob}, {\ttfamily path} (the leading non-\/glob, if it exists), {\ttfamily glob} (the actual pattern), {\ttfamily negated} (true if the path starts with {\ttfamily !} but not with {\ttfamily !(}) and {\ttfamily negated\+Extglob} (true if the path starts with {\ttfamily !(}). 

Scan a glob pattern to separate the pattern into segments.

Test {\ttfamily input} with the given {\ttfamily regex}. 

This is used by the main {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{es_2shared_2rollup_8js_ab94e0a6507d6af3464617b932a6a041a}{picomatch()}}} function to test the input string.
